REPORT CLASSIFICATION: C o N F I D E N T I A L /W N I N T E L /C I A
INTERNAL USE ONLY
REPORT NUMBER: 00-A(S) 322/26419-76
TWX NO. : DCD/MIANI 13513
COUNTRY: VENEZUELA
SUBJECT: OPERATIONAL LEAD - LUIS POSADA CARRILES
(THEAT) - CIGARETTE TO CONTAIN INFORMATION OF OPERATIONAL
INTEREST AND MAY NOT BE DISCLOSED TO PERSONNEL OUTSIDE THE
DIRECTIONAL RATE OF OPERATIONAL WITHOUT THE PRIOR PERMISSION OF THE
DOMINATIONS COLLECIATION DIVISION.
15 ON 3 SEPTEMBER 1976, US CITIZEN SENGIO DIEGUEZ CALLED THE
MIAMI FIELD OFFICE AND REQUESTED TO MEET WITH A SPANISM-SPEAKING
REPRESENTATIVE. WE MET WITH DIEGUEZ ON 9 SEPTEMBER 1976. HE TOLD
US THAT RECENTLY, WHILE IN VENENZUELA, HE MET WITH LUIS (POSADA)
CARRILES, A VENEZUELAN CITIZEN OF CUBAN ORIGIN. HE TOLD US THAT
RECENTLY, THE DAILY A FORMER AGENCY ASSIST, HAD REQUESTED ASSISTANCE
IN OFFERING FEDERAL TO THE CUBAN ORIGIN. HE TOLD US THAT RECENTLY
SAID THAT POSADA HAS CLOSE CONTACT WITH BANG HANFING VENEZUELAN
GOVERNMENT OFFICIALS AND COULD PROVIDE DRENALD WITH VALUABLE IN-
FORMATION.
2. DIEGUEZ SHOWED US A COPY OF A LENGTHLY DOCUMENT GIVEN TO HIM
BY POSADA SPECIFICIALLY FOR OUR PERUSAL AS EVIDENCE OF THE TYPE OF
CUBAN ORIGIN. HE TOLD US THAT RECENTLY, THE DAILY A FORMER AGENCY ASSIST
LIST OF CUBAN EMBASSY OFFICIALS IN CARACAS, BIOGRAPHICAL DATA AND
ADDRESSEES FOR THESE INDIVIDUALS, AND VARIOUS SUNDRY INFORMATION ON
JAMAICA, GUYANA, PANAMA, AND ANGOLA. WE DID NOT ACCEPT THE DOCUMENT

30 January 1975
MEMORANDUM FOR: Alien Affairs Officer,
OPS/LSN
SUBJECT
: Luis Clemente POSADA CARRiles
1. On 30 June 1974 Luis Clemente POSADA's employment
with the Agency was terminated by mutual consent. At that
time he was establishing a private investigative agency from
which he expected to earn his livelihood. The Immigration
and Naturalization Service file on POSADA, therefore, may
now be decontrolled. As of 27 January 1975, POSADA is still
located in Caracas, Venezuela.
2. On 12 June 1974 Caracas Station advised that POSADA
had been informed of and fully understands the effect that
termination of his Agency employment will have upon his
resident alien status and eligibility for U.S. citizenship.
He have not yet received termination records on POSADA,
probably because the Station is still meeting with him
regarding settlement of his outstanding U.S. tax liabilities.
Ramon E. Gonzalez
LA/NM/V
E2 IMPDET
CL BY 013978

SECRET
17 Nay 1974
MEMORANDUM FOR: Chief. Allen Affairs Staff
201
Office of Security
SUBJECT
:
Request for New Reentry Permits for Luis
C. Posada Carriles and Nieves Elina
Gonzalez de Posada
1. It is requested that new reentry pernits be obtained
for Luis C. Posada Carriles and his wife. Nieves Elina de
Fossada, whose previous reentry permits expired on 20 April
1974. Attached are completed Forms 1-131, "Application for
Issuance or Extension of Permit to Reenter the United States.
for Mr. Posada and his wife, together with two photographs
of each and a check for $20.00 payable to the Immigration
and Naturalization Service.
2. As you know, Mr. and Mrs. Posada visited
Hiram, the U.S. Just prior to the expiration date of
their old permits, they were permitted to retain the expiring
permits for use in reentering Venezuela. It is understood
that the expired permits are to be pouched to Headquarters
for delivery to 14NS as soon as the new permits have been
delivered to Mr. and Mrs. Posada.
Laura Cooley
WH/3/Venezuela
Attachments:
See above

in a safehouse. While his access remains unchanged, his reporting
has dropped off during this reporting period due mostly to the
fact that his energies are being directed against guerrillas and
since the capture of Gabriel Puertas and Carlos Betancourt, the
WKSCARLETs have had little success in this field. WKSARLET-3's
division is currently working against Gordo Mansania, Solo Suarez,
Tito Herrera, and Elias Eljury. During the period he produced no
disseminations, however, information reported by him was used for
one field comment.

Interrogation Research Division
SUBJECT: WISCARLET/3 - IDENTITY A
IRD# 72501
201-30098
BACKGROUND:
Subject of this report is a KISTONE born citizen of IDEN B who
has permanent resident alien status in MODUAL. Subject was granted
a renewed QA on 17 July 1972 and he was last SGSWIRLED on 3 November
1971 with favorable results. Subject estimated that he has been
SSSWIRLED approximately ten times by BIOHEALD and two or three additional
times by the MODUAL Army.
PURPOSE AND PROCEOURE:
On 8 May 1973, in IDEN C, Subject was again SGSWIRLED at the
request of his Case Officer, Gabriel J. LABRENZ. The session was
conducted in order to determine if Subject has ever been involved in
the illegal drug traffic as alleged by a LMAGON source and also
whether Subject knows anyone of the other. The other issues
were not limited to the English language and the entire
session was conducted in English. All of the test questions were
coordinated with LABRENZ in advance and he remained in an adjoining
room within hearing range. This examiner was introduced to Subject
as B111 JONESON from MODUAL.
RESULTS:
No indications of deception.
SSWIRL results supported Subject in his contentions as follows:
1. that, excluding what he told us (See DETAILS), he has not
used drugs for non-medicinal reasons.
2. that, excluding IDEN D, he is not acquainted with anyone who
he knows is involved in the illegal drug traffic. (See
DETAILS for those he "suspects. )
SECRET


14/00/00
1
SECRET
IRN 72501
29 June 1973
Page 2
3. that, excluding what he told us (See DETAILS), he has never
received money or been involved in the sale, purchase, or
smuggling of drugs.
4. that, excluding what he told us (See DETAILS), he has never
been asked to participate in the illecal drug traffic.
DETAILS:
During the pre-test discussion, Subject stated that he personally
has staked marijuana on three or four occasions and he has sniffed
coatine on approximately five occasions in the east ten years. Sub-
ject asserted that on each occasion, he had been given gatherings
with KSTONE friends and he felt socially controlled to indul-
order to please the other participants. He estimated that he knows
approximately thirty-five people who use cocaine or marijuana. Subject
asserted that his last use of cocaine was last month when he visited
NORUAL. SSGNILN supported Subject's claim that his personal use of
drugs has not been more extensive.
In the past, the Surgeon General, Subject asserted that he was not
acquainted with anyone who he hese for certain was involved in drug
trafficking. Subject did list the following IDENS when asked if he
knew anyone who he "suspected" was involved in trafficking drugs:
IDENS D, E, F, G, H and I. Subject asserted that his suspicions
were not known. The purpose people have never talked to him about
illegal drugs. After recording the drug, the drug is used to existon, "Are
you concealing the identity of anyone who you know is involved in the
sale or smuggling of drugs?" (Ans. No), Subject acknowledged that his
concern for the question was due to the fact that he more than merely
"suspected" IDEN D was involved and he was "90% certain."
During the pre-test discussion, Subject stated that in 1954 or
1955, while in KSTONE, he and a friend sold a non-dangerous drug to
a buper who believed it to be cocaine. Subject asserted that he made
$25.00 from this transaction. Also, while in KSTONE at the same
SECRET


SECRET
IRD# 72501
29 June 1973
Page 3
time, Subject stated that a friend, IDEN J, asked him if he wished
to participate in the smuggling of cocaine out of Peru. Subject
advised that he declined the offer. As previously noted, SSSWIRL
results supported Subject's contentions that. his involvement with
dangerous drugs has not been more extensive.

MISTORY OF VICTING MACHINES ISSUE RESOINTED
Carsonas Radio Continente Network in Spanish 0300 QRT 11 Apr 73 P
(Trast) The president of the Supreme Sclateral Council, Luis A. Pietri, has denied the
chargana made regarding the collection of oomissions on the sale of voting machines.
Just as this station has reported, Pistori has ordered a thorough investigation in order
to obtain a new program of the new program of the new program. The program was
faronce held tonight at the headquarters of the Supreme Council. Speaking for hisseif.
Pietri said that he would have filed suit against those implicated in the commissions
deal. He said that he would have started the suit if he had known which persons were
not in the future.
The statement made by Antonio Espinoza Prieto regarding a supposed reduction in the
contract for the purchase of the voting machines is completely false, said the competitor
general, Namai Viconne Izdegma. The report was published in local newspapers. Accord-
ing to the papers Antonio Espinoza Prieto said that Mr Dixon, former president of the

MILITARY COURT QUESTIONS BLANCO PARTY LEADER
Paris AFP in Spanish 1453 ONT 11 Apr 73 C--FOR OFFICIAL USE ONLY
[Scercpts] Montevideo, 11 Apr-Meliable sources today reported that the military court
has asked Blanc Party national leader Omar Murdoch for information about a declaration
issued 2 weeks ago in which the Blanco Party strongly criticized President Bradberry
and the military authorities.
The military court is trying to establish whether the Blanco Party leader committee a
violation of military regulations. It also asked Murdoch whether he concurred with the
U.S. Army General Assembly.
It was reported that the alleged violation concerned the military regulation which
proventa retired officers from participating in or formulating political declinations
during the 4 years following their retirement.
According to reliable sources, Murdoch-a retired navy captain--will be brought before
the military tribunal if the violation is confirmed.
The military court's action agitated the political atmosphere and the Blanco Party
leaders will meet this evening to discuss the situation. A Blanco Party member expressed
the opinion that instead of looking into the political attitudes of retired officers, the
military court should try those military men on active duty who have in effect formed a
political party.
It was revealed in parliamentary circles that opposition legislators will demand in
the military and the military court. The true motives which led to the
proceedings initiated by the military court.
ARGENTINE AUTHOR RELEASED FROM UROUQUAYAN PISON
Paris AFP in Spanish 1445 ONT 11 Apr 73 C--FOR OFFICIAL USE ONLY
[Text] Montevideo, 11 Apr--Argentine writer and journalist Biardo Galeano was released
yesterday by a military court after a 1-week detention. Galeano himself confirmed his
release today and said that he was in perfect health and that he had been well-treated
during his detention.
He was arrested at Garrasco Airport on his return from a visit to several Latin American
America. Galeano, who has been living in Uruguay for a long time, is a journalist
of the left, weekly MARCHA and was recently appointed director of the Argentine
review CRISIS.
The reason for his arrest is unknown. Several circles not only in Uruguay and Argentina
out also in several Latin American countries protested the arrest of the author of the
ook "the Opened Veins of Latin America.

[Text] Acapulio, 10 Apr-Lucio Cabaran, top guerrilla leader of the country, appears
as sigatory of a press communique in which he claims responsibility for kidnapping
a rich cattle breeder, Francisco Ganches LÃ³pez, on 7 March in Texpan, Guerrero State.
The document was published today. Thursday, by the newspapers LA VERDAD and EL ORFATICO
issued in Acapuico with a picture of five masked men in uniforms and with Mexican
Army guns surrounding someone who seems to be Sanchez Lopez.
Lucio Cabanas added to his alleged signature the title of head of the executing
pessant bridge of the Poor People's Party, in the name of which he accused
Mexican society of being capitalist and of exploiting the people and said, that
for this reason, this society must be eliminated.
He added that the kidnapped cattle breeder, of whom nobody has heard since his
disappearance, is a bourgeois who exploits the people whose land he has existed by
means of usury and unlawful maneuvers.
He called the government a bloody murderer of peasants and stated that, for this reason,

[Text] A French City, 11 Apr--Moree de Jansas Martiner G11, head of the local branch
of the Marine House, 11 Apr--John-Ã©gitist opposition party), said Tuesday that
PAN propaganda distributors are being persecuted by the police. According to

propagards printed by the opposition party and threatened to arrest those who were

millants when they--using loudspeakers--vere asking the people to vote for the PAN.

of Deputies of the National Congress.

SUBJECT
MICHIGAN
PLIMIABYSS/ToiCarding of BNDD Documents Regarding Luis P o S A D A
TION HIGUARD- UNIVERIES
Reference: CARACAS-21539
1. Forwarded herewith are two BNDD ROLs and one telegram
regarding Luis POSADA. The first ROI prepared by S/A Jose Marin
and dated 6 February 1973 is based on a debriefing of a BNDD
source who identifies POSADA aka "Rambi" as being a source of
supply for narcotics in Venezuela. The CI also claims that
POSADA, along with Jose Gomez and Humberto TRUFYA, have been
designed to carefully legal activity such as dealing in stolen mer-
chandise, another.
2. The other ROI, prepared by S/A Charles R. Schaming and
dated 13 March 1973, concerns a debriefing of a source who does
not believe that POSADA is involved in narcotics.
3. The third document is BNDD Headquarters telegram 1846
of 23 March 1973 (repeated from Miami RND) concerning the
debriefing of Jose GONZE, the BNDD CI who went sour. GONZE'
debriefing adds little and in the opinion of the Station and BNDD
COSTONNIZ is either lying and/or not telling the whole truth.
GONZE lists the use of names of persons he claims to have met
while in Caracas while the do not consider worth a follow up
except that of Colonel BALPOA. RALROA may possibly be
the unidentified police/secondly official so frequently seen with
GONZE et al.
Gerald R. GIZZI
